<a name="ps_1773900234615"></a>
## Prompt Set (ps_1773900234615)

**Time:** 2026-03-19T06:03:54.615Z
**Duration:** 0ms
**Tool Calls:** 1

### Text Exchange - 2026-03-19 06:03:54 UTC [07:03:54 CEST]

**Assistant Response:** PlantUML 1.2020.02 doesn't resolve `!include` relative to cwd OR the puml file location. It uses its own include path. The fix: use `!includesub` or pass `-Dincludes` flag, OR just use the absolute path in the puml file.
